# Task: Write Integration Tests for Flipt Evaluation API

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Output:** Write your integration test file to `/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go`

## Objective

Author integration tests for Flipt's feature flag evaluation REST API. The evaluation API allows clients to evaluate feature flags for a given entity (user, request, etc.) and receive a variant or boolean response.

## Scope

Explore the Flipt codebase to understand the evaluation API handlers. Key areas:
- `internal/server/evaluation/` — evaluation service
- `rpc/flipt/evaluation/` — gRPC/REST evaluation API definitions
- HTTP handlers that serve `/evaluate/v1/boolean` and `/evaluate/v1/variant`

Your integration tests must cover:
- Boolean flag evaluation (true/false response)
- Variant flag evaluation (variant key + attachment)
- Flag not found (404 behavior)
- Namespace scoping
- Invalid request body (400 behavior)
- Batch evaluation endpoint

## Output Format

Write a Go integration test file at:
```
/workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
```

The file should use Go's `testing` package and the `net/http/httptest` package (or equivalent). Each test function must start with `Test`.

## Quality Bar

- At least 6 test functions
- Each function has at least one `t.Fatal` / `t.Error` assertion
- Cover both success and error paths
- Do not fabricate API paths — inspect the actual codebase first
- Do NOT run the tests yourself — write the test file and the evaluation system validates independently

    23→func WithHTTPClient(client *http.Client) Option {
    24→	return func(t *Transport) { t.client = client }
    25→}
    26→
    27→func NewTransport(addr string, opts ...Option) Transport {
    28→	t := Transport{
    29→		client: &http.Client{Transport: http.DefaultTransport},
    30→		addr:   addr,
    31→	}
    32→	for _, opt := range opts {
    33→		opt(&t)
    34→	}
    35→	transport := t.client.Transport
    36→	t.client.Transport = roundTripFunc(func(r *http.Request) (*http.Response, error) {
    37→		md, ok := metadata.FromOutgoingContext(r.Context())
    38→		if ok {
    39→			if auth := md.Get("authorization"); len(auth) > 0 {
    40→				r.Header.Set("Authorization", auth[0])
    41→			}
    42→		}
    43→
    44→		return transport.RoundTrip(r)
    45→	})
    46→
    47→	return t
    48→}
    49→
    50→func checkResponse(resp *http.Response, v []byte) error {
    51→	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
    52→		var status status.Status
    53→		if err := protojson.Unmarshal(v, &status); err != nil {
    54→			return err
    55→		}
    56→		return status1.ErrorProto(&status)
    57→	}
    58→
    59→	return nil
    60→}

    13→// Storer is the minimal abstraction for interacting with the storage layer for evaluation.
    14→type Storer interface {
    15→	GetFlag(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error)
    16→	GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error)
    17→	GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, ruleID storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error)
    18→	GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, flag storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error)
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Server serves the Flipt evaluate v2 gRPC Server.
    22→type Server struct {
    23→	logger    *zap.Logger
    24→	store     Storer
    25→	evaluator *Evaluator
    26→	evaluation.UnimplementedEvaluationServiceServer
    27→}
    28→
    29→// New is constructs a new Server.
    30→func New(logger *zap.Logger, store Storer) *Server {
    31→	return &Server{
    32→		logger:    logger,
    33→		store:     store,
    34→		evaluator: NewEvaluator(logger, store),
    35→	}
    36→}
    37→
    38→// RegisterGRPC registers the EvaluateServer onto the provided gRPC Server.
    39→func (s *Server) RegisterGRPC(server *grpc.Server) {
    40→	evaluation.RegisterEvaluationServiceServer(server, s)
    41→}
    42→
    43→func (s *Server) AllowsNamespaceScopedAuthentication(ctx context.Context) bool {

   410→// ResourceRequest is used to identify a request predicated by revision, namespace and a key.
   411→// This is used for core resources (e.g. flag and segment) as well as to list sub-resources (e.g. rules and constraints).
   412→type ResourceRequest struct {
   413→	NamespaceRequest
   414→	Key string
   415→}
   416→
   417→// NewResource constructs and configures and new *ResourceRequest from the provided namespace and resource keys.
   418→// Optionally, the target storage revision reference can also be supplied.
   419→func NewResource(ns, key string, opts ...containers.Option[ReferenceRequest]) ResourceRequest {
   420→	p := ResourceRequest{
   421→		NamespaceRequest: NamespaceRequest{
   422→			key: ns,
   423→		},
   424→		Key: key,
   425→	}
   426→
   427→	containers.ApplyAll(&p.ReferenceRequest, opts...)
   428→
   429→	return p
   430→}
   431→
   432→// String returns a representation of the combined resource namespace and key separated by a '/'.
   433→func (p ResourceRequest) String() string {
   434→	return path.Join(p.Namespace(), p.Key)
   435→}

// NamespaceRequest is used to identify a request predicated by both a revision and a namespace.
// This is used to identify namespaces and list resources directly beneath them (e.g. flags and segments).
type NamespaceRequest struct {
	ReferenceRequest
	key string
}

// NewNamespace constructs a *NamespaceRequest from the provided key string.
// Optionally, the target storage revision reference can also be supplied.

func (s *Server) Batch(ctx context.Context, b *rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationRequest) (*rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse, error) {
	resp := &rpcevaluation.BatchEvaluationResponse{
		Responses: make([]*rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse, 0, len(b.Requests)),
	}

	for _, req := range b.GetRequests() {
		f, err := s.store.GetFlag(ctx, storage.NewResource(req.NamespaceKey, req.FlagKey, storage.WithReference(b.Reference)))
		if err != nil {
			var errnf errs.ErrNotFound
			if errors.As(err, &errnf) {
				eresp := &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse{
					Type: rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponseType_ERROR_EVALUATION_RESPONSE_TYPE,
					Response: &rpcevaluation.EvaluationResponse_ErrorResponse{
						ErrorResponse: &rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationResponse{
							FlagKey:      req.FlagKey,
							NamespaceKey: req.NamespaceKey,
							Reason:       rpcevaluation.ErrorEvaluationReason_NOT_FOUND_ERROR_EVALUATION_REASON,
						},
					},
				}

package integration_test

import (
	"bytes"
	"context"
	"encoding/json"
	"net/http"
	"net/http/httptest"
	"testing"

	"github.com/stretchr/testify/assert"
	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/server/evaluation"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/internal/storage"
	"go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt"
	rpcevaluation "go.flipt.io/flipt/rpc/flipt/evaluation"
	"go.uber.org/zap/zaptest"
	"google.golang.org/grpc"
	"google.golang.org/protobuf/encoding/protojson"
)

// MockEvaluationStore implements the Storer interface for testing.
type MockEvaluationStore struct {
	flags map[string]*flipt.Flag
	rules map[string][]*storage.EvaluationRule
}

func (m *MockEvaluationStore) String() string {
	return "mock"
}

func (m *MockEvaluationStore) GetFlag(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) (*flipt.Flag, error) {
	// Construct a key from namespace and flag key
	key := req.Key
	if ns := req.NamespaceKey; ns != "" {
		key = ns + ":" + key
	}

	flag, exists := m.flags[key]
	if !exists {
		return nil, storage.ErrNotFound(req.Key)
	}
	return flag, nil
}

func (m *MockEvaluationStore) GetEvaluationRules(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRule, error) {
	key := req.Key
	if ns := req.NamespaceKey; ns != "" {
		key = ns + ":" + key
	}
	rules, exists := m.rules[key]
	if !exists {
		return []*storage.EvaluationRule{}, nil
	}
	return rules, nil
}

func (m *MockEvaluationStore) GetEvaluationDistributions(ctx context.Context, req storage.IDRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationDistribution, error) {
	return []*storage.EvaluationDistribution{}, nil
}

func (m *MockEvaluationStore) GetEvaluationRollouts(ctx context.Context, req storage.ResourceRequest) ([]*storage.EvaluationRollout, error) {
	return []*storage.EvaluationRollout{}, nil
}

3. EDIT /workspace/integration/evaluation_integration_test.go
Before
// TestBooleanFlagEvaluationSuccess tests successful boolean flag evaluation.
func TestBooleanFlagEvaluationSuccess(t *testing.T) {
	// Create mock store with a boolean flag
	store := &MockEvaluationStore{
		flags: map[string]*flipt.Flag{
			"default:feature_flag": {
				NamespaceKey: "default",
				Key:          "feature_flag",
				Name:         "Feature Flag",
				Enabled:      true,
				Type:         flipt.FlagType_BOOLEAN_FLAG_TYPE,
			},
		},
		rules: map[string][]*storage.EvaluationRule{},
	}

	// Create evaluation server
	logger := zaptest.NewLogger(t)
	evalServer := evaluation.New(logger, store)

	// Create gRPC server to host the evaluation service
	grpcServer := grpc.NewServer()
	evalServer.RegisterGRPC(grpcServer)

	// Start test server (will use a listening socket)
	listener, err := net.Listen("tcp", "127.0.0.1:0")
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer listener.Close()

	go grpcServer.Serve(listener)
	defer grpcServer.Stop()

	// Create HTTP client pointing to the gRPC server
	conn, err := grpc.Dial(listener.Addr().String(), grpc.WithInsecure())
	require.NoError(t, err)
	defer conn.Close()

	// Create a simple HTTP handler that wraps the gRPC service
	handler := createEvaluationHTTPHandler(evalServer)

	// Create test HTTP server
	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
	defer server.Close()
After

// readBody reads the HTTP request body and returns it as bytes.
// If t is nil, it ignores errors; otherwise it fails the test on error.
func readBody(t *testing.T, r interface {
	Body interface {
		Read(p []byte) (n int, err error)
	}
}) []byte {
	var buf bytes.Buffer
	_, err := buf.ReadFrom(r.Body)
	if err != nil && t != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Failed to read body: %v", err)
	}
	return buf.Bytes()
}
After
// readBodyFromResponse reads the HTTP response body and returns it as bytes.
func readBodyFromResponse(t *testing.T, resp *http.Response) []byte {
	var buf bytes.Buffer
	_, err := buf.ReadFrom(resp.Body)
	if err != nil && t != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Failed to read response body: %v", err)
	}
	return buf.Bytes()
}

// readBodyFromRequest reads the HTTP request body and returns it as bytes.
func readBodyFromRequest(t *testing.T, req *http.Request) []byte {
	var buf bytes.Buffer
	_, err := buf.ReadFrom(req.Body)
	if err != nil && t != nil {
		t.Fatalf("Failed to read request body: %v", err)
	}
	return buf.Bytes()
}
